<h1 class="firstHeading" id="firstHeading" lang="en">List of computer science conferences</h1>
<div class="mw-body-content" id="bodyContent">
<div id="siteSub">From Wikipedia, the free encyclopedia</div>
<div id="contentSub"><span class="mw-redirectedfrom">  (Redirected from <a class="mw-redirect" href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_software_engineering_conferences&amp;redirect=no" title="List of software engineering conferences">List of software engineering conferences</a>)</span></div>
<div class="mw-jump" id="jump-to-nav">
					Jump to:					<a href="#mw-head">navigation</a>, 					<a href="#p-search">search</a>
</div>
<div class="mw-content-ltr" dir="ltr" id="mw-content-text" lang="en"><p>This is a list of <a href="/wiki/Academic_conference" title="Academic conference">academic conferences</a> in <a href="/wiki/Computer_science" title="Computer science">computer science</a>. Only established, well-known conferences are included; within each field; the conferences are ranked according to quality and impact. The ranking is approximate and non-authoritative.</p>
<p></p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="General">General</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_computer_science_conferences&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: General">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<ul>
<li>FCRC – <a href="/wiki/Federated_Computing_Research_Conference" title="Federated Computing Research Conference">Federated Computing Research Conference</a><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-fich-1996_1-0"><a href="#cite_note-fich-1996-1">[1]</a></sup></li>
</ul>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Algorithms_and_theory">Algorithms and theory</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_computer_science_conferences&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: Algorithms and theory">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="thumb tright">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:172px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:ESA_2009_coffee_break.JPG"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="1600" data-file-width="1067" height="255" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/6/64/ESA_2009_coffee_break.JPG/170px-ESA_2009_coffee_break.JPG" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/6/64/ESA_2009_coffee_break.JPG/255px-ESA_2009_coffee_break.JPG 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/6/64/ESA_2009_coffee_break.JPG/340px-ESA_2009_coffee_break.JPG 2x" width="170"/></a>
<div class="thumbcaption">
<div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:ESA_2009_coffee_break.JPG" title="Enlarge"></a></div>
<a href="/wiki/European_Symposium_on_Algorithms" title="European Symposium on Algorithms">ESA</a> 2009</div>
</div>
</div>
<div class="hatnote" role="note">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Theoretical_computer_science#Conferences" title="Theoretical computer science">Theoretical computer science § Conferences</a></div>
<p>Conferences accepting a broad range of topics from <a href="/wiki/Theoretical_computer_science" title="Theoretical computer science">theoretical computer science</a>, including <a href="/wiki/Algorithm" title="Algorithm">algorithms</a>, <a href="/wiki/Data_structure" title="Data structure">data structures</a>, <a href="/wiki/Computability" title="Computability">computability</a>, <a href="/wiki/Computational_complexity_theory" title="Computational complexity theory">computational complexity</a>, <a href="/wiki/Automata_theory" title="Automata theory">automata theory</a> and <a href="/wiki/Formal_language" title="Formal language">formal languages</a>:</p>
<ul>
<li>STOC – ACM <a href="/wiki/Symposium_on_Theory_of_Computing" title="Symposium on Theory of Computing">Symposium on Theory of Computing</a><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-era-a_2-0"><a href="#cite_note-era-a-2">[2]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-stoc-msas_3-0"><a href="#cite_note-stoc-msas-3">[3]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-citeseer100_4-0"><a href="#cite_note-citeseer100-4">[4]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-zaiane-other_5-0"><a href="#cite_note-zaiane-other-5">[5]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-stoc-arnet_6-0"><a href="#cite_note-stoc-arnet-6">[6]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-chazelle-1996_7-0"><a href="#cite_note-chazelle-1996-7">[7]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-georgiou-2007_8-0"><a href="#cite_note-georgiou-2007-8">[8]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-goldman-1999_9-0"><a href="#cite_note-goldman-1999-9">[9]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-jiang-1999_10-0"><a href="#cite_note-jiang-1999-10">[10]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-lynch-1996_11-0"><a href="#cite_note-lynch-1996-11">[11]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-navarro-2002_12-0"><a href="#cite_note-navarro-2002-12">[12]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-tel-2000_13-0"><a href="#cite_note-tel-2000-13">[13]</a></sup></li>
<li>FOCS – IEEE <a href="/wiki/Symposium_on_Foundations_of_Computer_Science" title="Symposium on Foundations of Computer Science">Symposium on Foundations of Computer Science</a><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-era-a_2-1"><a href="#cite_note-era-a-2">[2]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-zaiane-other_5-1"><a href="#cite_note-zaiane-other-5">[5]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-chazelle-1996_7-1"><a href="#cite_note-chazelle-1996-7">[7]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-georgiou-2007_8-1"><a href="#cite_note-georgiou-2007-8">[8]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-goldman-1999_9-1"><a href="#cite_note-goldman-1999-9">[9]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-jiang-1999_10-1"><a href="#cite_note-jiang-1999-10">[10]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-lynch-1996_11-1"><a href="#cite_note-lynch-1996-11">[11]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-navarro-2002_12-1"><a href="#cite_note-navarro-2002-12">[12]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-tel-2000_13-1"><a href="#cite_note-tel-2000-13">[13]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-focs-msas_14-0"><a href="#cite_note-focs-msas-14">[14]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-focs-arnet_15-0"><a href="#cite_note-focs-arnet-15">[15]</a></sup></li>
<li>ICALP – <a href="/wiki/International_Colloquium_on_Automata,_Languages_and_Programming" title="International Colloquium on Automata, Languages and Programming">International Colloquium on Automata, Languages and Programming</a><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-era-a_2-2"><a href="#cite_note-era-a-2">[2]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-zaiane-other_5-2"><a href="#cite_note-zaiane-other-5">[5]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-chazelle-1996_7-2"><a href="#cite_note-chazelle-1996-7">[7]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-jiang-1999_10-2"><a href="#cite_note-jiang-1999-10">[10]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-navarro-2002_12-2"><a href="#cite_note-navarro-2002-12">[12]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-icalp-msas_16-0"><a href="#cite_note-icalp-msas-16">[16]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-icalp-arnet_17-0"><a href="#cite_note-icalp-arnet-17">[17]</a></sup></li>
<li>STACS – <a href="/wiki/Symposium_on_Theoretical_Aspects_of_Computer_Science" title="Symposium on Theoretical Aspects of Computer Science">Symposium on Theoretical Aspects of Computer Science</a><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-jiang-1999_10-3"><a href="#cite_note-jiang-1999-10">[10]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-navarro-2002_12-3"><a href="#cite_note-navarro-2002-12">[12]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-stacs-msas_18-0"><a href="#cite_note-stacs-msas-18">[18]</a></sup></li>
<li>ISAAC – <a href="/wiki/International_Symposium_on_Algorithms_and_Computation" title="International Symposium on Algorithms and Computation">International Symposium on Algorithms and Computation</a><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-era-a_2-3"><a href="#cite_note-era-a-2">[2]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-chazelle-1996_7-3"><a href="#cite_note-chazelle-1996-7">[7]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-navarro-2002_12-4"><a href="#cite_note-navarro-2002-12">[12]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-isaac-msas_19-0"><a href="#cite_note-isaac-msas-19">[19]</a></sup></li>
<li>MFCS – <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=International_Symposium_on_Mathematical_Foundations_of_Computer_Science&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="International Symposium on Mathematical Foundations of Computer Science (page does not exist)">International Symposium on Mathematical Foundations of Computer Science</a><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-era-a_2-4"><a href="#cite_note-era-a-2">[2]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-jiang-1999_10-4"><a href="#cite_note-jiang-1999-10">[10]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-navarro-2002_12-5"><a href="#cite_note-navarro-2002-12">[12]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-mfcs-msas_20-0"><a href="#cite_note-mfcs-msas-20">[20]</a></sup></li>
<li>FSTTCS – IARCS <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Conference_on_Foundations_of_Software_Technology_and_Theoretical_Computer_Science&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Conference on Foundations of Software Technology and Theoretical Computer Science (page does not exist)">Conference on Foundations of Software Technology and Theoretical Computer Science</a><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-navarro-2002_12-6"><a href="#cite_note-navarro-2002-12">[12]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-fsttcs-msas_21-0"><a href="#cite_note-fsttcs-msas-21">[21]</a></sup></li>
<li>FCT – <a href="/wiki/International_Symposium_on_Fundamentals_of_Computation_Theory" title="International Symposium on Fundamentals of Computation Theory">International Symposium on Fundamentals of Computation Theory</a><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-fct-msas_22-0"><a href="#cite_note-fct-msas-22">[22]</a></sup></li>
<li>COCOON – <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=International_Computing_and_Combinatorics_Conference&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="International Computing and Combinatorics Conference (page does not exist)">International Computing and Combinatorics Conference</a><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-era-a_2-5"><a href="#cite_note-era-a-2">[2]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-navarro-2002_12-7"><a href="#cite_note-navarro-2002-12">[12]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-cocoon-msas_23-0"><a href="#cite_note-cocoon-msas-23">[23]</a></sup></li>
<li>WoLLIC – <a href="/wiki/Workshop_on_Logic,_Language,_Information_and_Computation" title="Workshop on Logic, Language, Information and Computation">Workshop on Logic, Language, Information and Computation</a><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-reasoner_24-0"><a href="#cite_note-reasoner-24">[24]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-wollic-msas_25-0"><a href="#cite_note-wollic-msas-25">[25]</a></sup></li>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Algorithms">Algorithms</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_computer_science_conferences&amp;action=edit&amp;section=3" title="Edit section: Algorithms">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Conferences whose topic is <a href="/wiki/Algorithm" title="Algorithm">algorithms</a> and <a href="/wiki/Data_structure" title="Data structure">data structures</a> considered broadly, but that do not include other areas of theoretical computer science such as computational complexity theory:</p>

<li>WADS – <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Algorithms_and_Data_Structures_Symposium" title="Algorithms and Data Structures Symposium">Algorithms and Data Structures Symposium</a><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-era-a_2-8"><a href="#cite_note-era-a-2">[2]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-chazelle-1996_7-6"><a href="#cite_note-chazelle-1996-7">[7]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-navarro-2002_12-10"><a href="#cite_note-navarro-2002-12">[12]</a></sup></li>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Operating_systems">Operating systems</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_computer_science_conferences&amp;action=edit&amp;section=13" title="Edit section: Operating systems">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>

CRC Press. <a href="/wiki/International_Standard_Book_Number" title="International Standard Book Number">ISBN</a> <a href="/wiki/Special:BookSources/0-8493-2649-4" title="Special:BookSources/0-8493-2649-4">0-8493-2649-4</a>.</cite><span class="Z3988" title="ctx_ver=Z39.88-2004&amp;rfr_id=info%3Asid%2Fen.wikipedia.org%3AList+of+computer+science+conferences&amp;rft.atitle=Computational+learning+theory&amp;rft.aufirst=Sally+A.&amp;rft.aulast=Goldman&amp;rft.btitle=Algorithms+and+Theory+of+Computation+Handbook&amp;rft.date=1999&amp;rft.genre=bookitem&amp;rft.isbn=0-8493-2649-4&amp;rft.pub=CRC+Press&amp;rft_val_fmt=info%3Aofi%2Ffmt%3Akev%3Amtx%3Abook"><span style="display:none;"> </span></span>.</li>
<li><cite class="citation book" id="CITEREFHincheyBowenRouff2005"><a href="/wiki/Michael_Hinchey" title="Michael Hinchey">Hinchey, Michael</a>; <a href="/wiki/Jonathan_Bowen" title="Jonathan Bowen">Bowen, Jonathan P.</a>; Rouff, Christopher A. (2005). "Introduction to formal methods". In Rouff, Christopher A.; Hinchey, Michael; Rash, James; Truszkowski, Walter; Gordon-Spears, Diana. <i>Agent Technology from a Formal Perspective</i>. Springer. pp. 25–64. <a href="/wiki/International_Standard_Book_Number" title="International Standard Book Number">ISBN</a> <a href="/wiki/Special:BookSources/978-1-85233-947-0" title="Special:BookSources/978-1-85233-947-0">978-1-85233-947-0</a>.</cite><span class="Z3988" title="ctx_ver=Z39.88-2004&amp;rfr_id=info%3Asid%2Fen.wikipedia.org%3AList+of+computer+science+conferences&amp;rft.atitle=Introduction+to+formal+methods&amp;rft.au=Bowen%2C+Jonathan+P.&amp;rft.aufirst=Michael&amp;rft.aulast=Hinchey&amp;rft.au=Rouff%2C+Christopher+A.&amp;rft.btitle=Agent+Technology+from+a+Formal+Perspective&amp;rft.date=2005&amp;rft.genre=bookitem&amp;rft.isbn=978-1-85233-947-0&amp;rft.pages=25-64&amp;rft.pub=Springer&amp;rft_val_fmt=info%3Aofi%2Ffmt%3Akev%3Amtx%3Abook"><span style="display:none;"> </span></span>.</li>
<li><cite class="citation book" id="CITEREFJiangLiRavikumar1999">Jiang, Tao; Li, Ming; Ravikumar, Bala (1999). "Basic notions in computational complexity". In <a href="/wiki/Mikhail_Atallah" title="Mikhail Atallah">Atallah, Mikhail J.</a> <i>Algorithms and Theory of Computation Handbook</i>. CRC Press. <a href="/wiki/International_Standard_Book_Number" title="International Standard Book Number">ISBN</a> <a href="/wiki/Special:BookSources/0-8493-2649-4" title="Special:BookSources/0-8493-2649-4">0-8493-2649-4</a>.</cite><span class="Z3988" title="ctx_ver=Z39.88-2004&amp;rfr_id=info%3Asid%2Fen.wikipedia.org%3AList+of+computer+science+conferences&amp;rft.atitle=Basic+notions+in+computational+complexity&amp;rft.aufirst=Tao&amp;rft.aulast=Jiang&amp;rft.au=Li%2C+Ming&amp;rft.au=Ravikumar%2C+Bala&amp;rft.btitle=Algorithms+and+Theory+of+Computation+Handbook&amp;rft.date=1999&amp;rft.genre=bookitem&amp;rft.isbn=0-8493-2649-4&amp;rft.pub=CRC+Press&amp;rft_val_fmt=info%3Aofi%2Ffmt%3Akev%3Amtx%3Abook"><span style="display:none;"> </span></span>.</li>
<li><cite class="citation book" id="CITEREFMutzelEades2002"><a href="/wiki/Petra_Mutzel" title="Petra Mutzel">Mutzel, Petra</a>; <a href="/wiki/Peter_Eades" title="Peter Eades">Eades, Peter</a> (2002). "Graphs in software visualization". <i>International Dagstuhl Seminar on Software Visualization, May 2001, Revised Papers</i>. <a href="/wiki/Lecture_Notes_in_Computer_Science" title="Lecture Notes in Computer Science">Lecture Notes in Computer Science</a>. <b>2269</b>. Springer. pp. 285–294. <a href="/wiki/Digital_object_identifier" title="Digital object identifier">doi</a>:<a class="external text" href="//dx.doi.org/10.1007%2F3-540-45875-1_22" rel="nofollow">10.1007/3-540-45875-1_22</a>. <a href="/wiki/International_Standard_Book_Number" title="International Standard Book Number">ISBN</a> <a href="/wiki/Special:BookSources/978-3-540-43323-1" title="Special:BookSources/978-3-540-43323-1">978-3-540-43323-1</a>.</cite><span class="Z3988" title="ctx_ver=Z39.88-2004&amp;rfr_id=info%3Asid%2Fen.wikipedia.org%3AList+of+computer+science+conferences&amp;rft.atitle=Graphs+in+software+visualization&amp;rft.au=Eades%2C+Peter&amp;rft.aufirst=Petra&amp;rft.aulast=Mutzel&amp;rft.btitle=International+Dagstuhl+Seminar+on+Software+Visualization%2C+May+2001%2C+Revised+Papers&amp;rft.date=2002&amp;rft.genre=bookitem&amp;rft_id=info%3Adoi%2F10.1007%2F3-540-45875-1_22&amp;rft.isbn=978-3-540-43323-1&amp;rft.pages=285-294&amp;rft.pub=Springer&amp;rft.series=Lecture+Notes+in+Computer+Science&amp;rft_val_fmt=info%3Aofi%2Ffmt%3Akev%3Amtx%3Abook"><span style="display:none;"> </span></span>.</li>
<li><cite class="citation book" id="CITEREFOvermars1998"><a href="/wiki/Mark_Overmars" title="Mark Overmars">Overmars, Mark H.</a> (1998). "Geometric algorithms for robotic manipulation". <i><a href="/wiki/International_Colloquium_on_Automata,_Languages_and_Programming" title="International Colloquium on Automata, Languages and Programming">International Colloquium on Automata, Languages and Programming</a></i>. Lecture Notes in Computer Science. <b>1443</b>. Springer-Verlag. pp. 116–117. <a href="/wiki/Digital_object_identifier" title="Digital object identifier">doi</a>:<a class="external text" href="//dx.doi.org/10.1007%2FBFb0055045" rel="nofollow">10.1007/BFb0055045</a>. <a href="/wiki/International_Standard_Book_Number" title="International Standard Book Number">ISBN</a> <a href="/wiki/Special:BookSources/3-540-64781-3" title="Special:BookSources/3-540-64781-3">3-540-64781-3</a>.</cite><span class="Z3988" title="ctx_ver=Z39.88-2004&amp;rfr_id=info%3Asid%2Fen.wikipedia.org%3AList+of+computer+science+conferences&amp;rft.atitle=Geometric+algorithms+for+robotic+manipulation&amp;rft.aufirst=Mark+H.&amp;rft.aulast=Overmars&amp;rft.btitle=International+Colloquium+on+Automata%2C+Languages+and+Programming&amp;rft.date=1998&amp;rft.genre=bookitem&amp;rft_id=info%3Adoi%2F10.1007%2FBFb0055045&amp;rft.isbn=3-540-64781-3&amp;rft.pages=116-117&amp;rft.pub=Springer-Verlag&amp;rft.series=Lecture+Notes+in+Computer+Science&amp;rft_val_fmt=info%3Aofi%2Ffmt%3Akev%3Amtx%3Abook"><span style="display:none;"> </span></span>.</li>
<li><cite class="citation book" id="CITEREFSamet2010">Samet, Hanan (2010). "Multidimensional data structures for spatial applications". In Atallah, Mikhail J.; Blanton, Marina. <i>Algorithms and Theory of Computation Handbook</i> (2nd ed.). CRC Press. <a href="/wiki/International_Standard_Book_Number" title="International Standard Book Number">ISBN</a> <a href="/wiki/Special:BookSources/978-1-58488-822-2" title="Special:BookSources/978-1-58488-822-2">978-1-58488-822-2</a>.</cite><span class="Z3988" title="ctx_ver=Z39.88-2004&amp;rfr_id=info%3Asid%2Fen.wikipedia.org%3AList+of+computer+science+conferences&amp;rft.atitle=Multidimensional+data+structures+for+spatial+applications&amp;rft.aufirst=Hanan&amp;rft.aulast=Samet&amp;rft.btitle=Algorithms+and+Theory+of+Computation+Handbook&amp;rft.date=2010&amp;rft.edition=2nd&amp;rft.genre=bookitem&amp;rft.isbn=978-1-58488-822-2&amp;rft.pub=CRC+Press&amp;rft_val_fmt=info%3Aofi%2Ffmt%3Akev%3Amtx%3Abook"><span style="display:none;"> </span></span>.</li>
<li><cite class="citation web" id="PODCmailinglist"><a class="external text" href="http://www.podc.org/podc-mailinglist.txt" rel="nofollow">"PODC mailing list"</a>. <i><a href="/wiki/Symposium_on_Principles_of_Distributed_Computing" title="Symposium on Principles of Distributed Computing">PODC</a></i><span class="reference-accessdate">.
